Important News

Documents Regarding the Wanbaoshan Incident Negotiations Between China and Japan (2)

Agreement Personally Made Between the Japanese Consul and the Municipal Chief 79

On June 8th, the Japanese Consul in Changchun, Toshiro Tashiro, met with Zhou Yuping to discuss the issue of investigating the Korean people's farming of rice paddies and digging irrigation channels in Wanbaoshan. The following temporary agreement was concluded in person: (1) Both Chinese and Japanese police will immediately withdraw; (2) The dispute between the Korean people and the local farmers will be investigated on-site by representatives from both sides, and mediators from both sides will be invited to assist in the investigation. After the facts of the case have been fully investigated, it will be resolved in accordance with fair and best practices; (3) The Korean people there shall immediately stop digging and building the canal leading to the Yitong River; (4) After the case is resolved, the Korean people there will then separately decide whether to stay or leave. Before the case is resolved, during the period when the Korean people have ceased work, the Changchun County Public Security Bureau shall be responsible for their protection, and the current state of affairs that have already been worked on shall not be changed temporarily; (5) After the investigation of this case is completed, it will be resolved by both parties in the shortest possible time.

Letter from the Municipal Government to the Japanese Consul 80

Dear Sir, your official document No. 38 of June 6th has been received and respectfully read. This dispute is of the utmost importance to the majority of landlords and farmers. The ownership of the land by the landlords and farmers there is a legitimate and inherent right. Regarding the work currently being carried out by the Korean people to channel water from the Yitong River, it is necessary to investigate on-site whether there is a consensual agreement between both parties, and how this work is causing damage to the landlords and farmers, in order to seek a fair and just resolution. Regarding the agreement reached between us yesterday that both parties' police will withdraw at the same time, the Korean people will stop work, and both parties will send representatives to conduct on-site investigations together, and then an appropriate resolution will be made. In accordance with the preceding reasons in your letter, a corresponding letter is hereby sent in reply for your review. To: Resident Japanese Consul in Changchun, Toshiro Tashiro, June 9th.

Letter from the Municipal Government to the Japanese Consul 81

Dear Sir, Regarding the case of the Korean people in Wanbaoshan cultivating rice paddies and digging waterways, which both parties have sent representatives to investigate on-site, it is now reported that the personnel from our office who went to investigate together have returned to the office with a report. A corresponding report of the factual situation is sent for your review. To: Resident Japanese Consul in Changchun, Toshiro Tashiro, attached investigation report, one copy (omitted), June 11th.

Letter from the Municipal Government to the Japanese Consul 82

The Changchun Municipal Government, after the representatives of both parties jointly conducted an on-site investigation in Wanbaoshan, proved that the Korean people's planned waterway cannot be tolerated. Unexpectedly, the Korean people continued the waterway work, which led to a conflict between the two parties. The chief of the office sent a letter to the Japanese Consul on June 11th, giving a final warning, and stated that if the Japanese Consul still does not accommodate, then all disputes and losses that occur in the future shall be borne by the Japanese side. The full text has already been seen in this newspaper on July 9th, and will not be repeated.

Facts of the Joint Chinese and Japanese Investigation 83

The Changchun Municipal Government, together with the Japanese side, investigated the results of the Korean people forcibly digging the waterway in Wanbaoshan on June 11th. The full text of the reports submitted by both parties has been seen in this newspaper on June 18th, omitted. (to be continued)

After Chinese Residents in Korea Sought Refuge in Andong 84

Foreign Affairs Support Council Resolved Eight Items

Accommodating Over Three Thousand Three Hundred People

All Circles Enthusiastically Relieving Refugees

Andong Correspondence: Chinese residents in Korea, unable to withstand the oppression of the rioters, have been returning to Andong in droves to seek refuge in recent days. The Andong County Government, together with the Public Security Bureau and the General Chamber of Commerce, are working hard to find ways to provide relief. Various entertainment venues in the city have been borrowed and converted into shelters. As of noon on the 10th, a total of 2,881 refugees have been accommodated. In addition, people from all walks of life have been generously donating to help the refugees. Moreover, Japanese merchants in Chinese Street, such as Dalian Steamship Company, Shimizu Yoko, Xiecheng Bank, Manchuria Bank, Fukuzo Yoko, etc., have voluntarily donated 30 to 50 yuan each, in order to ease the tension with the Chinese side. The National Foreign Affairs Support Council of this port held

Meetings repeatedly in recent days, and voted on eight items: (1) To issue a comforting declaration to the citizens of this port; (2) To advise citizens to proceed along the right track and avoid exaggerated propaganda that deviates from the facts; (3) To resolve to inform the whole country of the tragic situation of the riot; (4) To telegraph to the provincial and higher authorities to report the actual situation and request instructions; (5) To send representatives from the association to the shelters to comfort the refugees; (6) To send representatives from the association to be responsible for investigating the course of the tragedy and collect various materials; (7) To inquire with the provincial association about its stance on the riots and request that it order all branches to act in unison; (8) To request that the authorities appoint appropriate personnel to go to the site of the incident to conduct a thorough investigation of the losses of the Chinese people, in order to demand compensation. This afternoon, Mr. Han Jinghai, chairman of the Sinuiju Chamber of Commerce, came to Andong and met with the local authorities to report that Consul Zhu of Sinuiju had made serious representations to the Japanese side. The governor of Pyeonganbuk-do replied that the Korean people would not take such actions again. The Japanese authorities in Sinuiju also made the same statement verbally. County Magistrate Wang Jie'an believed that this verbal statement was not sufficient and requested a written guarantee, but was not granted. It can be seen that they have no sincerity in protecting them.

Another correspondence: Since the riots throughout Korea, Chinese residents in Korea have been fleeing to Andong in droves. However, because Korean people gathered on the Yalu River Bridge to obstruct and beat them, many have been crossing on sampans in the river. From the morning of the 7th to the evening of the 10th, the stream has not stopped. The violence of the Korean rioters has not yet ended, but has decreased somewhat in the last day or two compared to the 7th and 8th. Since this case occurred, the market in Andong has been extremely turbulent, and the atmosphere has suddenly become tense. Every day the streets are crowded with pedestrians, especially near the Japanese concession in Qidaogou. Heavy guard posts have been added to the Sino-Japanese border, and the city's merchant corps has also been fully mobilized to suppress the unrest. Moreover, because the theaters and cinemas are all full of refugees, all entertainment venues in the city have been closed down, presenting a rather unique phenomenon. However, all the small restaurants are making three times their usual profit, and although the inns are full of refugees, because they have fled alone, they are unable to pay for room and board. In recent days, the Japanese telegraph office has banned sending telegrams about this case, and the Japanese post office has also strictly checked the passengers on the Chinese-Korean route, and they must pass through inspection before being allowed to pass. The number of refugees currently being accommodated locally is roughly as follows: Refugees Temporary First Shelter, Dan Gui Stage, 1,200 people; Second Shelter, Xin Ming Stage, 569 people; Third Northeast Cinema, 410 people; Fourth Dong Ping Cinema, 317 people; Fifth Dong Ming Cinema, 385 people. All of the above five shelters are under the responsibility of the Public Security Bureau for day and night protection. In addition, there are 91 refugees at Yulai Inn, 40 at Desheng Lou, 145 at Fengshun Inn, 130 at Yuluan Company, and 43 at Heshun Yuan. Excluding those who have relied on relatives and friends, there are a total of over 3,300 refugees (the above is the number counted up to the 10th). Before the negotiations are properly resolved, they can only be temporarily accommodated here. Moreover, the people of the city are voluntarily donating money and assisting with steamed buns in an unusually enthusiastic manner. Sun Guangyu Tang, a wealthy gentleman in the city, donated 120 yuan. County Government Chairman Wang Jiegong, Commercial Port Public Security Bureau Chief Zhang Hanwei, Chamber of Commerce Chairman Sun Langxuan, and Yucheng Hao, Jiang Chunbo, etc., each donated 100 yuan. Up to the afternoon of the 10th, it is estimated that over 2,100 yuan has been received in donations, and over 30,000 steamed buns (11th).

Overseas Chinese in Tokyo and Toyama Attacked by Koreans 85

Osaka Correspondence: Recently, incidents of Koreans attacking and beating Overseas Chinese in the Japanese mainland have occurred from time to time. The Japanese government does not take measures to suppress the violence of the Koreans. At 9:00 PM on the 10th of this month, the home of Overseas Chinese Fang Renli, who lives in Toyama City near Tokyo, was suddenly broken into by Koreans wielding iron bars and other weapons, who completely destroyed the furniture and injured Fang and others. At around 11:00 PM, another five or six Koreans came to commit violence again. The Fang family was attacked twice in one night, and everything was completely destroyed. Fortunately, during the second act of violence, more than a dozen Japanese police officers arrived and arrested one Korean, who is currently being held in the Toyama Station for questioning. The Korean's name is Kim Bok-bu, and he is a construction worker (July 11th).

Case of American Hospital in Dezhou Shooting and Killing a Chinese Person 86

The Murderer is the Deputy Superintendent, American DeForest

The County Magistrate and the Local Court have Examined the Corpse and Taken Photographs

Han Fuju Ordered the Secretariat to Investigate in Detail and Handle the Case

Jinan Correspondence: To the east of Dezhou City, in Dongdi, there is the Weishi Boji Hospital, which is run by the church. The location is grand, and the equipment is also very comprehensive. However, the foreigners in the hospital are extremely violent. Very few people from De County seek medical treatment there. Most of those who are treated every day are their religious followers. At around 5:00 AM on the 11th, the Deputy Superintendent of the hospital, American DeForest, suddenly shot and killed Wang Guoqing, a Chinese worker in the hospital. Due to serious injuries, he died soon after. At that time, the hospital kept it strictly secret and refused to tell anyone. Therefore, it was not until the 12th that De County Magistrate Li Shude and others received a report. They immediately went to the hospital early that morning, together with Court President Wang of the local court, Prosecutor Sun, Committee Member Wang of the County Party Affairs Reorganization Committee, and the chiefs of the Education, Public Security, Finance, and Construction Bureaus, to examine the body of Wang Guoqing. It was found that Wang Guoqing's body was covered in blood, and he had been shot in the lower back, resulting in serious injuries and death. The bullet that entered had not been taken out. A photo was immediately taken for evidence. As for the reason why American DeForest shot and killed Wang Guoqing, the hospital was evasive and the details are still unknown. Today (13th), De County Magistrate Li Shude sent a telegram to Jinan, separately to Chairman Han Fuju and Civil Affairs Director Li Shuchun, reporting everything. Han immediately instructed the secretariat to investigate the truth and then handle the case. At the same time, Wu Zhenzuan, President of the High Court, also received a telegram from the De County Local Court, and the Shandong Provincial Reorganization Committee also received a telegram from the County Party Department. All circles in Jinan are shocked and outraged that the American dared to arbitrarily shoot and kill a Chinese person in the interior of our country, and his violence can be said to be extreme. The telegram from De County Magistrate Li Shude to Chairman Han and Civil Affairs Director Li is included below: "To Chairman Han and Civil Affairs Director Li: At around 5:00 AM this morning, American DeForest, Deputy Superintendent of the Weishi Boji Hospital of the church in our county, shot and killed Wang Guoqing, a Chinese worker in the hospital, who died shortly afterwards. The county magistrate heard the news this morning and went to examine the body with Court President Wang, Prosecutor Sun, Committee Member Mao of the County Department, and the chiefs of the bureaus. It was found that he was injured in the lower back, and the bullet had entered but not exited. A photograph was taken immediately. In addition to waiting for the cause to be ascertained, a detailed report will be sent separately. Respectfully reported, Official Li Shude bowed." (13th)

Communist Bandits in Western Jiangxi Defeated One After Another 87

The Kong Gang Fled to the Border of Hunan and Hubei

The Li Gang Fled to the Vicinity of Xinfeng

Nanchang Correspondence: The border area of ​​Hunan, Hubei, and Jiangxi to the west of the Gan River was originally a den of Communist bandits. After the Zhu, Mao, Peng, and Huang gangs concentrated on the east bank of the Gan River, those in western Jiangxi, including Kong Hechong's pseudo-Independent Division, Li Shixing's pseudo-16th Army, Liu Tiechao's pseudo-20th Army, and Li Mingrui's pseudo-7th Army, were scattered in Yongxin, Jinlian, Lotus, Tonggu, Wanzai, and the Pingliu, Linggui, and Yangxin areas of Hunan, and the Shixi area of ​​Hubei. They drifted and were unpredictable, sometimes in Hunan, sometimes in Hubei, and sometimes in Jiangxi. Yesterday, according to a victory report from the Yifeng Office, on the 7th of this month, Kong Hechong's pseudo-4th Brigade held a welcoming meeting for the pseudo-Soviet Provincial Government Committee on Tianbao Mountain (the bandit nest of Yifeng Tonggu). The pseudo-79th and 2 divisions also rushed from the border of Hunan to participate. After learning the news, the Suppression of Communist bandits army stationed in Yifeng immediately organized a team and rushed to attack. The bandit army resisted stubbornly. After eight hours of fierce fighting, the Suppression of Communist bandits army finally broke through the bandit's position and occupied Tianbao. The remnants of the bandits fled into the mountains on the border of Hunan and Hubei. Hundreds of bandits were killed in this battle, dozens were captured, and dozens of guns were seized. The Li Mingrui gang on the Hunan-Jiangxi border recently entered Guidong and Lingxian of Hunan from Lotus. Because the Hunan East Army fiercely encircled and suppressed them, they re-entered Ganzhou from Chongyi Shangyou, attempting to attack Ganzhou City. Fortunately, the Ma brigade had prepared in advance, and the bandits failed to succeed. It is said that they have fled south to the Xinfeng area. As for the Liu bandits and Zeng Bingchun and other small gangs who harassed the Yuan River and appeared in Xinyu, Xiajiang, and Fenyi, they have more than a thousand guns. They have also been severely suppressed by the Zhu brigade and suffered heavy losses. They have no power. In addition, Yongxin, Ninggang, and Lianhua, which are on the border of Hunan, have been occupied by bandits for three years. The tragic situation is difficult to describe. The bandit leaders are still unknown, and they are mostly local peasant bandits and vagrants. There are very few guns. After the large gangs in southern Jiangxi are suppressed, these small gangs will not be enough to quell (July 13th).

Compilation of Progress of the Suppression of Communist Bandits Army 88

The Right Wing Encircled and Attacked Donggu

The Left Wing Went Straight to Guangchang

The Central Route Recovered Zhaoxie

Nanchang Correspondence: The Suppression of Communist Bandits Army has been attacking the various bandit nests for days, with the momentum of breaking bamboo. Now, the situation is compiled as follows:

The Right Wing Recovered Futian 89

Futian, 60 miles south of Ji'an, is located between Jishui and Taihe. Its terrain is dangerous and is the location of the Red Bandit's Pseudo Provincial Government. After capturing Wangtian, the various armies of the Right Wing of the Suppression of Communist Bandits Army divided into routes to capture Futian. The bandits immediately withdrew to Donggu (60 miles from Futian). The Suppression of Communist Bandits Army occupied Futian on the 10th and searched many important documents of the Red Bandits in the bandit den, which roughly stated that we (the bandits call themselves) should quickly withdraw the various departments due to strategic considerations, leaving the old and weak to guard Donggu and reorganizing the strong into Fujian. From this, we can see the strategy and discouragement of the Red Bandits. After the Right Wing Army captured Futian, they searched and advanced towards Donggu, encircling Donggu and limiting it to be recovered before the 15th. Also, our army has cleared the bandits in Shuikou, Shuinan, and Baisha and arrived at Luofang.

Our Army Destroyed Xingtan 90

This place has recently received a telegram from Commander Hao, roughly stating that our army occupied Xingtan Yanfang today and captured more than a hundred peasant bandits. The remnants of the bandits fled to the old nest. According to the bandits who were captured, the pseudo-Soviet Provincial Government was originally in Xingtan, with two to three hundred guns and more than 500 bandits. Since Tengtian was occupied by the National Army, the bandit officials of the pseudo-Provincial Government were all panic-stricken and fled in all directions.

The Central Route Advanced to Ningu 91

Sun Lianzhong reported on the 9th of the Central Route Army that our Dong brigade occupied Dongbei at Gengchen, and the bandits collapsed towards the Dongbianling Houfang Tanghou. Li Brigade Yuyu occupied Xinfeng at Wushi, seized more than 20 guns, and killed about 300 bandits. Capturing more than 30 people, the remnants of the bandits, the pseudo-3rd Army 9th Division Commander Lu Yangang and 37th Division Commander Chen Bojun, collapsed to the southeast. It is said that they have a plan to retreat to Luokou Longgang. At the same time, Gao Division of the same army corps once again broke through the important bandit nest of Zhaoxie in Le'an, opening the throat into Ningdu. Gao's department then attacked Dongshao Luokou of Ningdu. According to reconnaissance reports, the large gangs of armed bandits in those two places had already withdrawn, and only small gangs of Red Bandits were covering the retreat, and they were about to retreat to Ningdu City. Dongshao Luokou will be captured in a matter of days. This is the gateway to Ningdu City, and with this, Ningdu should not be a problem.

Guangchang is About to be Recaptured 92

When the Left Wing of the Suppression of Communist Bandits Army advanced from Nanfeng to Guangchang, the bandits in the various bandit nests on the Nangguang border, such as Xiaotian and Qiacun, had all fled at the sight of the army. Therefore, after the Suppression of Communist Bandits Army arrived at Baishui, they immediately copied south of Guangcheng, advancing south from Qiacun Kuzhu, and directly approaching Dongshao, so Guangchang City is not a problem. As for the Suppression of Communist Bandits Army after capturing Lichuan, they have arrived at Deshengguan, the border of Shaowu Chengchuan. The bandits in Guangze and Shaowu have collapsed to Ninghua Changting.

The Plight of the Red Bandits 93

The Red Bandits were originally divided into three front armies, under the jurisdiction of more than a dozen pseudo-armies and several independent divisions. However, they all focused on burning and killing. Since Chiang himself supervised the encirclement and suppression of the army, the Red Bandits were extremely terrified. Now, the confessions of the bandits obtained by the various armies are extracted as follows to see one aspect: Gao Shuxun's gray telegram stated that according to a bandit scout's confession, the main force of the bandits had fled to the border between Fujian and Jiangxi. Now, due to the pressure from the National Army, they have changed their strategy, and Zhu Mao has ordered all the bandits to gather in Donggu within six days in order to survive. Shangguan Yunxiang's telegram stated that according to the confession of a surrendered bandit company commander, the elite troops of the Red Bandits have all been sent to the Fujian border to plunder food and transport it back to their old nest in order to defend it to the death. However, the Red Bandits are good at attacking but not good at defending. If the National Army strikes with full force, they can be completely eliminated.

Commander Chiang Orders Establishment of Prisoner-of-War Camps 94

Commander-in-Chief Chiang, considering the large number of captured Red bandits from various armies, and especially the pitiable plight of coerced peasant bandits, has specifically ordered the Chief Commanders of the left and right wings, He and Chen, and Chief of Staff Xiong, to establish prisoner-of-war reception camps in Nanfeng, Nancheng, Ji'an, and Nanchang. This is to accommodate and reform them. The Party and Government Committee is currently actively preparing for this. (July 13th)

Zhang Jingyao Returns Documents from Hunan Province 95

Totaling More Than Thirty Sheets

Changsha Correspondence: During Zhang Jingyao's tenure as governor of Hunan, he aggressively extorted wealth. Afterwards, he even absconded with Hunanese property, causing significant losses to public and private assets in Hunan Province. Recently, when Shao Lizi went north, Zhang ingratiated himself and, during their conversation, surprisingly produced a large package of land and property deeds from the former Hankou branch of the Hunan Bank, which he had seized during his time as governor. The package contained over thirty sheets. His intention was to curry favor, but also because the properties covered by the deeds were all located in Hankou, making them impossible to manage. These deeds have now been taken back to the province by Zhang Muxian, director of the Fourth Route Army Headquarters' office in Beijing, and handed over to the Finance Department for verification. It is reported that the Finance Department considers the deeds returned by Zhang to be only a portion of the total and plans to send another letter requesting the return of the remainder for proper arrangement. As for the thirty-odd deeds returned this time, the Finance Department has already instructed Tao Bingyi, the Hunan property administrator in Hubei, to inspect and verify them according to the deeds. The instruction reads: "It has been found that the title deeds for the Hunan Bank property in Hankou, previously managed by this department, were all taken away by Zhang Jingyao in the ninth year of the Republic. Yesterday, Zhang Muxian, director of the Fourth Route Army Headquarters' office in Beijing, handed over several property deeds from Zhang Jingyao's returned property in Hankou. After the handover, a copy of the addresses and names of the deeds is enclosed. You are to inspect and verify them for record. Furthermore, upon checking the two deeds for Zhuanwa Lane listed in the attached sheet, there is still a piece of land that was negotiated but could not be recovered. Also, there is no record in this department for a plot of land at Huangjiadun Dadangzi. Please investigate and recover it, and report the findings for verification." (July 7th)

Enthusiastic Efforts by Various Sectors in Guangdong to Raise Funds for Flood Relief 96

Organizations and Groups Have Dispatched Relief Teams on Separate Routes

The Fundraising Office is Renamed the All-Sectors Flood Relief Association

Guangzhou Correspondence: The massive floods in the three rivers of Guangdong Province have caused severe devastation. In recent days, the upstream of the West River has continued to breach dikes. Because the West River is receding very slowly, the water level at Sanshui Southwest was sixteen feet and two inches deep on the morning of the eighth, receding nine inches in the afternoon. The dikes upstream have been saturated for days, and collapse is feared. Currently, villagers near the dikes are conscripting workers day and night for rescue efforts, which are extremely busy. However, due to insufficient rescue efforts, some dikes have already collapsed, including the Wutang Dike in the Sixth District of Gaoyao County and the Sanzhou Dike in Gaoming County, with breaches of hundreds of feet. In addition, the Nan'an, Xiaoling, Baihe, and Junzhou dikes have collapsed successively, with breaches of hundreds or dozens of feet. Currently, the disaster areas in the northwest and west rivers are vast, and disaster-stricken groups are sending over ten telegrams daily appealing for relief. The Chamber of Commerce, charitable organizations, and hospitals established a fundraising office some days ago, immediately forming the first and second emergency relief teams. The Fangbian Hospital and the city Chamber of Commerce each advanced 5,000 yuan to purchase grain for distribution in the Beijiang areas of Yingde, Yuantan, Sanshui, and Qingyuan. The relief team arrived in Sanshui on the afternoon of the seventh and then proceeded to Sihui before heading to Qingyuan and Yingde. The third and fourth teams departed on the eighth on the Fumin and Xin'an ships, with a total of over sixty team members, carrying 56,000 catties of rice donated by the Hong Kong Po Tao Hall and a large quantity of medicines donated by various pharmacies. They set off for the disaster areas in Qingyuan and Qingjiang. The fifth relief team is scheduled to depart on the tenth aboard two merchant ships for Sanshui and Sihui. Also, the Tung Wah Hospital of Hong Kong and the Nanyang Company have transported a large quantity of rice and formed a relief team that will join in the distribution on the seventh and eighth. On the ninth, the group sent out thirty more personnel with thirty-nine boxes of biscuits and one hundred bags of rice aboard two merchant ships and the Xinping steamship, departing for areas under Sanshui, Lubao, Sihui, and Qingyuan. Ten-odd relief workers from the Provincial Civil Affairs Department set out on the morning of the eighth at ten o'clock, along with officials from the River Management Office, to provide disaster relief and investigate the situation in the disaster areas along the way, carrying a large quantity of grain and over ten loads of cakes and miscellaneous grains. These relief workers have arrived at their destinations one after another, distributing relief separately and conducting on-the-ground investigations. The authorities recently ordered the allocation of 50,000 yuan for relief distribution, which can be delivered to the Civil Affairs Department during the day for distribution. In addition, donors include Hong Kong merchants who donated 1,000 yuan, the Shipping Association which donated 2,000 catties of rice, and another 5,000 catties of relief rice from Hong Kong which will arrive today. Compatriots from Qingyuan residing in the province have appointed fundraising specialists to solicit donations in various places and arrange for disaster-stricken residents of the county to come to the province for admission to the pauper education and care home. The fundraising office established by the business and charitable sectors a few days ago yesterday resolved to rename itself the Guangdong Flood Relief Association, jointly organized by the business and charitable sectors, and invited representatives from the political and media sectors to join in the charitable cause. Zou Lu was publicly elected as the chairman of the relief association, which is divided into four departments: general affairs, fundraising, relief affairs, and public relations. Each department has subordinate publicity and entertainment sections to facilitate operations. (July 10th)

Flooding in Counties Along the Huai River in Northern Anhui 97

Disaster Situation is Extremely Severe, Refugees Cry Out for Food

Bengbu Red Swastika Society Appeals on Behalf of Disaster Victims

Bengbu Correspondence: Northern Anhui has suffered repeatedly from banditry, and the people's livelihood has not yet been eased. Everyone hoped for a bumper harvest this autumn to recover and breathe, but in recent days, continuous rain has caused rivers to flood, not only destroying the autumn harvest but also collapsing houses and leaving people homeless. Alas, the disaster victims have nowhere to die. The surge in the Huai River's water level is actually due to the rise of the Three Rivers Tip in the upper reaches due to heavy rain. Counties along the Huai River have mostly become wetlands, and the disaster situation is more severe than in the tenth year of the Republic. Recently, Fuyang County alone has had 50,000 households flooded, with over 2,000 disaster victims drowned and a large number of livestock killed. The northern border of Huoqiu is entirely under water, and fields of grain have all been flooded. Disaster victims are coming east in groups to escape the disaster, and those passing through the area these days are endless, sleeping in the wind and eating in the dew, in a miserable state. The county has suffered both the Red disaster and now the flood disaster, which is truly tragic. The city wall of Shouxian is close to the Huai River. With days of torrential rain, the river overflowed, and a foot of the city wall was washed away. Residents inside the city are rushing to rebuild while blocking the four gates to prevent flooding. Yingshang and Fengtai counties, due to their proximity to the Huai River, have raging floods, and villages on both sides of the river are flooded, and the disaster can be imagined. Huaiyuan County is located at the confluence of the Wo and Huai Rivers, which is a crucial point. Due to the continuous heavy rain, the two rivers have overflowed in recent days, and the area within dozens of miles is a vast expanse of water. Within the old city, boats travel on level ground, and villages outside the city have mostly become wetlands. Suxian County suffered a terrible hail disaster last month, and recently, the northwest area of the county has also experienced severe flooding, with all of the autumn harvest being submerged. The disaster victims in Bengbu have been provided with emergency relief by local organizations and groups, and enough donations will be raised within days to begin distribution. In the area of Wuhe County, downstream of the Huai River, a flood control dike was destroyed by torrential rain, and water flowed outward, destroying many riverside villages. In Xuyi County, the floods have been severe, and the water is vast. The disaster is also extremely severe. Along the upper and lower reaches of the Huai River, fields and crops have been damaged and submerged, and the autumn harvest will definitely be greatly reduced. The Bengbu branch of the World Red Swastika Society believes that the floods in the counties along the Huai River are extremely tragic and that relief should be sought. On the 11th and 12th, they telegraphed the National Government, the Anhui Provincial Government, the Central Relief Committee, the Anhui Relief Committee, and the Red Swastika Societies in Beijing, Ping, and Hangzhou, reporting the flood situation in northern Anhui and appealing on behalf of the disaster victims, requesting the allocation of funds for relief. Also, when the Huai River was experiencing torrential rain and rising floodwaters the other day, the water flow was rapid, and navigation was dangerous. Small short- and long-distance passenger ferries were temporarily suspended. Since the 12th, the weather has cleared, and the water level has gradually receded, and the small ferries have resumed normal operations. (July 13th)

Robbery in the Second District 100

In Pengzhuang Village, fifteenth neighborhood, second district of this county, the homes of Gao Lian'gen, Gao Ziqing, and Li Yinxiang were suddenly visited by more than ten robbers, speaking in local and Jiangbei dialects, armed with long guns and carrying shoulder poles. Chuansha

Tight Security in Hengsha, Sixth District 101

Hengsha, the sixth district under Chuansha County, is isolated on the coast, and pirates often covet it. To prevent such occurrences, the people of the district organized a defense force two years ago, engaging in training to deter threats. Recently, they have added a large number of firearms, increasing their strength, and set up sentry posts at various ports and main roads, rotating on duty. Anyone with suspicious behavior will be inspected.

Changshu

Wind Blows Down Prison Wall 102

On the twelfth of this month, there was a strong wind and heavy rain here, lasting for a full day and night. Not only did the water rise in the river, but many dilapidated houses and utility poles were also damaged. The west prison in the old county market had been built for a long time and was in poor condition. Because the new prison was under construction, repairs had been neglected. Unexpectedly, after this rainstorm, the water inside accumulated to more than a foot. On the twelfth, a strong wind caused the wall of the number one cell in the south of the prison to collapse with a loud crash, startling the guards and prisoners. Fortunately, the wall fell outward, and no prisoners were injured. After checking the prisoners, there were no escapes. The guards immediately moved the prisoners from the damaged cell to another cell and quickly reported to the public security substation, requesting that police be sent to suppress any unrest. The next day, Fan Qi, the chief of the substation, submitted a report to the county government on the damage to the wall and immediately expedited repairs to prevent accidents.

Jinjiang Ferry Damaged 103

Since the continuous rain, low-lying areas have become wetlands, and villages have reported the disaster situation to the county government. Unexpectedly, there was another wind and rainstorm on the twelfth, lasting a full day and night, causing the water to rise several more feet. Farmers were building dikes and trying to pump water out of the fields, but they were hit again, causing great hardship to the villagers. As for transportation, it could have been restored in three days, but now it will be extended again. However, the ferry companies are only interested in profit and are still secretly operating. Some are even traveling secretly at night, which the villagers cannot prevent, causing significant damage to the dikes in the Wuta area. Therefore, Zhang Dekang, the head of the district, upon the villagers' repeated requests, has petitioned the county government, requesting that it order the ferry companies to stop operating the ferries. Also, the Jinjiang Ferry of the Huitong Company, carrying passengers, tried to come to Changshu from Suzhou on the morning of the thirteenth. To avoid the villagers' mischief, it detoured into Yangcheng Lake. Unexpectedly, when the ferry came out of Hengjingtang, it was spotted by villagers, who gathered dozens of people and surrounded the Jinjiang Ferry with several small boats, intending to destroy its machinery. The bookkeeper and others tried their best to dissuade them and offered to pay the farmers 20 yuan for the dike construction fee, which calmed the situation down. Unexpectedly, before it had traveled even a mile, it was stopped again. After pleading and slowly passing through, it was again stopped near Zhangjiadian, where more farmers had gathered and insisted on stopping. The ferry personnel pleaded as before, but the farmers ignored them. Soon, dozens of people surrounded the ferry and used yellow stones and wooden sticks to beat it, resulting in the destruction of the glass windows on both sides and a large hole in the bow of the ship. At this point, the passengers were terrified and agreed to hire a private boat back to Changshu. The Jinjiang Ferry remained there. Fortunately, the passengers were unharmed. In the southern village, the disaster situation has been reported to the county by the seventh district farmers' association, requesting that personnel be sent to investigate.

Education Representatives Petition to the Department 107

The Wuyi County Education Administration Conference decided that the education budget for the 20th year of the Republic had a shortfall of 60,000 yuan that could not be made up, so it was decided that all education funding, except for community education funding, would be issued at 90% of the original amount, and the balance would be made up after revenue was received. If this decision became a reality, the schools would face many difficulties. At the joint county-school conference, it was unanimously agreed to protest and appoint Zhuang Ruzhen, Chen Hua, and Jiang Mianzhai as representatives to petition the department not to approve the decision. On the 14th, the three representatives went to the province by car and submitted their petition. Yang, the department director, met with them. After the three representatives presented their views, Director Yang acknowledged that issuing 90% of the funding was not a proper method and advocated starting with increasing revenue to remedy the situation. If the county really had no other way, then education was a sacrifice, and they would only be advised to try their best. However, the education bureau had not yet submitted the proposal to the department, so the department had no record to go on. The three representatives had to leave and return to Changzhou. A meeting will be held on the 17th to discuss what attitude to take after this.

Armed Villagers Open Dikes, Militia Fires Shots 117

The land in Nanzao, Juegang, is low-lying. Severe Flooding in Liyang 118

Since the beginning of summer, Liyang has had continuous rain for ten days, and the river water has risen several feet. Low-lying areas have become wetlands, and dikes have been washed away. The weather cleared on the previous two days, and there was still some hope for the higher fields, but unexpectedly, dark clouds gathered again last night, and the heavy rain continued throughout the night without stopping. The city streets were ankle-deep in water, and the seedlings in the higher fields were also submerged, with a vast expanse of water everywhere. The flooding this year is even worse than in the thirty-second year of the Guangxu Emperor. Even if the weather clears immediately, it will be difficult to salvage the situation. In this situation, famine is inevitable, and the autumn harvest is hopeless. Hangzhou

Inside Story of Meyfarth's Property Sale 122

The Englishman Meyfarth has resided in Hangzhou for several decades under the guise of missionary work and medical practice. During the Northern Expedition in Zhejiang in the sixteenth year of the Republic, all his properties were confiscated. Recently, Meyfarth, believing that the circumstances have changed, has been actively seeking their return. Considering that foreigners owning property inland is prohibited by treaty, it is tentatively permitted to sell the properties to Chinese individuals at a fair price. However, Meyfarth has a considerable number of henchmen, including those who willingly flatter foreigners like slaves, who are acting as fronts to take over the purchases. Rumors are spreading, causing public outcry. The Provincial Relief Institute once petitioned to have the properties allocated to the institute as a fund. Shangyu

Banditry in Siming Mountain 123

Following the resurgence of bandit activity in Pingkeng and Huixi villages along the border between Yu and Feng, banditry in Siming Mountain has also erupted. The area, bordering Sheng and Feng counties, is characterized by a continuous mountain range extending over a hundred li, renowned as a natural stronghold. Bandits have occupied this territory. Recently, bandit groups from Xinchang and Sheng counties, having been severely suppressed by the Sixth Regiment of the Peace Preservation Corps, have fled to Siming Mountain, engaging in arson, kidnapping, and the rape of women, escalating the situation. Wealthy families in nearby villages have relocated, while many impoverished residents have aligned themselves with the bandits. The mere mention of the area evokes fear and suspicion. Recently, a certain Mi from Dongjia'an and a certain Dong from Xiahuang village in Sheng county were kidnapped by bandits, who sent letters demanding ransom.

Hefei

Hefei Flooded 124

Recent continuous heavy rains have caused the Chicken Crowing and Siding mountains in the west to flood eastward, while the inland river tides of Lake Chao have surged westward. The torrential downpour over the past week has resulted in water backing up into the city. The areas around Xiaodongmen, Xiaoyaojin, Jiushiqiao, and Wanshou Palace have been transformed into a watery expanse. Collapsed walls and houses are common, and reports of people being crushed and killed are frequent. Outside Xiaodongmen, entire households are submerged. The area around Dawangmiao, Zhougudui, and the southeastern villages extending over ten li is completely flooded. Numerous village houses have collapsed, leaving victims exposed on higher ground and in boats, presenting a scene of utter misery. The households on the embankment of the foreign docks outside Dadongmen are also submerged. The Li Xiaowei and Da Yaowan attached to the city have been breached. All the small Sunjia, Cheng Ma, and Huli embankments along the lake and river have collapsed. The most fortified Dongda embankment is also in imminent danger. The Hefei-Wuhu small steamer has temporarily suspended service since the 7th due to obstructions to the embankment. The Hefei-Chao and Hefei-Bengbu buses have also temporarily suspended operations due to road damage. The county government today ordered the embankment chiefs of the remaining intact embankments to oversee the urgent construction and reinforcement of the embankments. However, most of the crops have already been ruined. The unprecedented fire in Hefei has not even been a month ago, and now this ruthless flood has occurred, truly a case of misfortunes never coming singly.

Correspondence

Letter from the Eighth Detachment, Second District, Zhejiang Inland River Police Bureau 125

To the Editor:

Having read your newspaper's local news report of the 12th of this month concerning the "Misunderstanding of Jiashan Xitang Water Police Seizing Opium," there are discrepancies between the report and the facts. Upon investigation, on the afternoon of the 8th of this month, a patrol from our detachment was dispatched to the well-known opium den of Yang Xin'guan (also known as Yang San'guan) on Xijie Street in this town to apprehend opium offenders. It happened that Lu Baozhi, the district chief of the Third District of Jiashan, was smoking opium in the den. Upon seeing the police enter the building, he hastily jumped out the back window and fled. The water police, recognizing the escaping individual as a district chief, believed it would affect their reputation and did not pursue him. At the time, only the den owner, Yang Xin'guan, was arrested, along with a straw hat left behind by Mr. Lu, and they were turned over to the Jiashan County Court for investigation. As for our detective Xu Gang (also known as Xu Mazi), due to a false accusation, he was indeed suddenly arrested by the Fifth Company of the Second Regiment of the Jiangsu Security Corps on the morning of the 1st of this month. After investigation by the Bandit Suppression Headquarters stationed in Songjiang, Jinshan, and Jiashan, it was confirmed that he was falsely accused, and he was released and returned to the detachment on the 11th of this month, resuming his duties as usual. The arrest of opium offenders and the arrest of our detective are two separate issues, with no connection between them. Moreover, the district office and the Yang surname opium den are located in Nan Hai and Xijie Street respectively, separated by a considerable distance across the river and street. If District Chief Lu Baozhi had not been illegally smoking opium in the den, our detachment would not have involved him without reason. We are sending this letter specifically so that your newspaper may investigate and publish a correction, thereby clarifying the facts.

The Eighth Detachment, Second District, Zhejiang Inland River Police

July 14th

Educational News

Important News

Amendment to Regulations for Overseas Chinese Students Returning to China for Education 126

The Ministry of Education has amended six articles of the Regulations for Overseas Chinese Students Returning to China for Education, which were promulgated on the 14th. (Article 1) Overseas Chinese students intending to return to China for education should request their guardians or former schools to seek guidance from the relevant consulate or local educational organization, and obtain a letter of introduction containing the following information: 1. Name, 2. Gender, 3. Age, 4. Native place, 5. Education, 6. Guardian's name and occupation, 7. Personal photograph. (Article 2) Overseas Chinese students returning to China for education should first contact the educational administrative authority at their destination, requesting an introduction to apply to a school and enroll in a suitable class. (Article 3) Provincial and municipal education departments should provide practical guidance to Overseas Chinese students returning to China for education. In areas with a higher concentration of returning Overseas Chinese students (such as Tianjin, Shanghai, Xiamen, Shantou, Guangzhou, etc.), personnel should be assigned specifically to handle these matters. (Article 4) Overseas Chinese students returning to China for education who, after passing the entrance examination, are deemed to have insufficient academic level for admission should be handled by the school or local educational administrative authority, considering the circumstances, according to the following measures: 1. The school shall independently provide opportunities for remedial study. 2. Introduce them to schools with a comparable academic level or schools with Overseas Chinese remedial classes. (Article 5) Overseas Chinese students returning to China for education whose family circumstances are certified as impoverished by the relevant consulate or a registered Overseas Chinese educational organization may be granted a waiver of tuition fees by the school they are attending, at its discretion. (Article 6) These regulations shall be implemented upon approval and promulgation by the Minister of Education.

Private Middle Schools Approved and Registered by the Ministry of Education in June 127

The Ministry of Education has issued a notice to the provincial and municipal education departments and the Weihaiwei Management Office regarding the list of private middle schools and school boards approved and registered in June, as follows:

(Jiangsu) Nantong College Affiliated Middle School, Wuxi Jiangnan Junior Middle School, Zhenjiang Chongshi Girls' Middle School, (Hebei) Bojing Sichen Junior Middle School, (Hunan) Changsha Miaogaofeng Middle School, Changde Hanwen Junior Middle School, (Guangdong) Guangzhou Dazhong Middle School, (Zhejiang) Shaoxing Junde Girls' Junior Middle School, Yuecai Junior Middle School, (Beiping) Yuhua Junior Middle School, (Shanghai) Chengzhong Middle School, Nanyang Model Junior Middle School, Aiqun Zizi Junior Middle School, Bowen Girls' Junior Middle School, Huzhou Luhu Junior Middle School, Peiming Girls' Middle School, Yucai Junior Middle School, Nanyang Middle School, Mailun Middle School, Minli Middle School, Nanyang Girls' Middle School, Guanghua University Affiliated Middle School, Junyi Middle School, Qianye Junior Middle School, Zhengfeng Middle School, Fudan Experimental Middle School, Shibei Middle School, Chizhi College Affiliated Middle School.

Sports

Jiangnan Northern Expedition Triumphant Return 130

| Arrived in Shanghai at 7:30 AM Yesterday |

Victorious in Repeated Battles, Awe-Inspiring in Tianjin and Beiping

Regret Over Inability to Go to Liaoning

The Jiangnan Northern Expedition Track and Field Team returned triumphantly at 7:30 AM yesterday morning. They defeated the Central team in Nanjing, Tianjin in the north, and Luhu in Beiping, achieving three victories in three battles, which is highly commendable. However, stopping in Tianjin and Beiping and not being able to go through the pass and shake hands with Liaoning and Shenyang is a matter of utmost regret for all the athletes. They hold it in their hearts, and can only wait to meet again at the National Games. Yesterday, I met with the team leader, Wang Fudan, to discuss the situation of the expedition as follows:

Northern Expedition Negotiation Process 131

The Jiangnan Track and Field Team's Northern Expedition plan was formulated as early as early June. On June 10th, the Sports Association sent letters to Zhang Boling in Tianjin, Ma Yuehan in Beiping, and Hao Gengsheng in Shenyang. Tianjin replied by telegram, expressing a sincere welcome to compete and immediately began preparations. Beiping stated that it lacked organization and it would be difficult to have a competition. Ma Yuehan was then requested to use his best efforts to mediate. The Liaoning side stated that due to the major examinations, the competition could only be held on July 5th. As the team had made this arrangement, it was scheduled to go north on the 24th. However, due to the issue of the Ma Lingsi match, the departure was delayed until the 27th, assuming that they would be able to catch the Shenyang competition on July 5th.

Reasons for Inability to Go to Shenyang 132

The Northern Expedition team arrived in Tianjin on the 30th. Heavy rain was pouring down. There were concerns that they would miss the Shenyang date, so there was a proposal to go through the pass first and then return to Tianjin and Beiping. Suddenly, news came that the two universities in Liaoning province were holding major examinations and needed until the 9th to finish. In this case, there was still plenty of time, so a quick letter was sent to Hao Gengsheng to inform him. One side telegraphed Zhang Lingjia, reporting the date of the trip to Shenyang. Unexpectedly, like a bolt out of the blue, a quick letter was received from Hao stating that the Association in Shanghai had not telegraphed back to confirm the date, and that the Northeast University team was going to Harbin for practice, so the competition could only be cancelled. The Tianjin side felt that since an agreement had been made beforehand, this sudden cancellation was suspicious. Later, it was learned that the Northeast team did not depart until the 17th. The entire team felt deeply regretful that the Northeast could not have practice competitions. An excerpt from Hao's original letter is as follows: "However, because the universities are currently undergoing major examinations, the competition can only be held on July 5th. Earlier or later dates are inconvenient. I then telegraphed the Shanghai National Association for approval. It has been ten days, and there has been no reply. On the evening of the 26th of last month, I sent a telegram to Mr. Shen Siliang in my personal capacity. Yesterday, I received a letter from the Association stating that the team is about to leave. (Omission) Please convey to the team that the confrontation in Liaoning is practically impossible because no official response was received for a long time."

Disappointment in Beiping 133

After the competition in Tianjin, they immediately went to Beiping. Beiping lacked organization and could not compete, so they leisurely toured the scenic spots and waited for several days. There was an alliance with Luhu to negotiate a competition. Luhu was the strongest team in Beiping, and no one could compete with them. Jiangnan won against them. According to Luhu, they had been preparing for a long time, but initially thought that Beiping would have an official team to compete. Unfortunately, this was not the case, so Luhu came out to fight.

Best Impression of Tianjin 134

The best impression of the Northern Expedition was Tianjin. They were the most energetic, and the facilities and hospitality were excellent. The team members were all in good health. A total of three people did not return. Wang Zhengyin returned to Shenyang, Ma Fengrui was in Tai'an, and Zhou Ende stayed in Tianjin. The rest returned together. They are determined to practice hard and prepare to compete against strong enemies at the National Games.

The Basketball King of the Three Islands 138

Among Japanese university basketball teams, the University of Commerce, Rikkyo, and Waseda have been the strongest for seven years, and the University of Commerce has been the leader among the three. The university basketball combined competition only started in 1924. The three schools joined at that time. Two years later, Teidai and Chuo joined one after another to form a five-way alliance. The 1926, 1927, 1929, and 1930 championships all went to the University of Commerce. The Jingu Athletic Stadium stone monument commemorates this. This spring, the Philippine Santo Tomas team went to Japan, and although it lost to the University of Commerce, the score was very close.

Far Eastern Athletes as Coaches 139

The head coach, Ohashi, and the assistant coach, Ueda, were both athletes in last spring's Far Eastern Games, playing forward. Both are students at the University of Commerce and were appointed as head and assistant coaches after graduating this year. There must be elite soldiers under good generals. In the Eighth Far Eastern Games, there were six team members from the University of Commerce in the Japanese team. In last spring's Ninth Far Eastern Games, there were three, including Ohashi and Ueda. Ohashi and his comrades had a great deal of credit for the ability to beat the Philippines and China last year. It is predicted that Japan will be represented by the University of Commerce at the Tenth Far Eastern Games.

Two Coaches Will Show Their Skills 140

Ohashi and Ueda will participate in performances in Shanghai. If it is a school-to-school match, they will provide guidance. If it is not a school but an organization, they will take the field and show their skills.

Free Talk

World Tidbits 158

— Hai Ke

Research on Lips

There is a professor in Germany who has conducted in-depth scientific research on human lips. According to him, the structure of each person's lips is closely related to their personality. It is not only related to personality, but also to occupation. For example, the female operators in telephone companies often have full and extremely soft lips, and the sounds they utter are solid and extremely clear. In the world, all foolish and barbaric races have very thick lips. Those famous great thinkers all have thin lips. However, there are some uncivilized and ignorant savage races whose lips are also thin. Therefore, the world is so big that there is nothing strange. Even in the case of lips, there cannot be a general conclusion.

The Water of the Ganges

Indians call their Ganges River the Holy River. The water in the Ganges is also regarded as fairy water. It is beneficial to the human body to drink it. Therefore, ordinary men and women of faith are happy to drink the fairy water. Recently, scientists have tested it and found that the mold in the river does have the ability to kill many kinds of germs. Look at the turbidity of the river water, which is obviously unsanitary. Who knew that there would be such a special mold, which made those scientists very suspicious. The Tropical School of Medicine in Calcutta has studied it in detail. It is said that if this kind of mold is artificially propagated, it can be used for medical treatment in the future.

A Tragic and Enthusiastic Aid-Overseas Chinese Assembly 159

— Sun Choucheng

All circles in this city, because of the inhumane massacre of overseas Chinese by Koreans, held a meeting at the Shanghai Chamber of Commerce on the 13th of this month to discuss countermeasures.

A Glimpse of the Venue: The national flag of the Kuomintang was hung high at the gate. Armed guards stood on the left and right. The scene was very solemn. The venue was in the conference hall on the second floor. A registration desk was set up at the entrance. After signing in, each person was given a printed item, "An Appeal to Compatriots of All Circles in the Country by Fellow Koreans in Shanghai," which contained titles such as "The Heartbreaking Korean Anti-Chinese Activities," "The Extremely Dangerous Situation of Overseas Chinese," "The Cruel Killing 丨丨 Dissecting Hearts and Gouging Out Eyes," "The Dangerous Violence 丨丨 Burning and Looting," "Overseas Chinese Seeking Refuge Are Massed Like Mountains and About to Run Out of Food," and "The Situation Is Deteriorating Day by Day and Is Precarious," which made it unbearable to read.

Various Slogans: This Korean riot was entirely instigated by the Japanese. Therefore, the slogans posted inside and outside the venue on that day were all directed at Japan. Excerpts are as follows: "The Wanbaoshan Incident was a Premeditated Conspiracy by the Japanese," "Demand That the Government Implement Revolutionary Diplomacy," "The Wanbaoshan Incident is an Excuse for the Japanese to Send Troops to the Northeast," "Compatriots, Rise Up and Destroy This Korea," "The Wanbaoshan Incident is a Prelude to the Japanese Aggression of Manchuria and Mongolia," "National Crisis Has Arrived, Compatriots, Wake Up Quickly," "All Circles Unite to Confront Japan as a Diplomatic Backing," "With a Spirit of Perseverance and Courage, We Will Forever Break Off Economic Relations with Japan."

Weeping Bitterly: Mr. Yang, an overseas Chinese from Japan, reported on the Japanese conspiracy against China, speaking in Cantonese. He said with great anger that he had been in Japan for more than ten years and had been in contact with the Japanese, knowing that they had been plotting against China with ulterior motives. It is difficult to describe their sinister methods in one word. The Koreans have always succumbed to the accumulated power of Japan and have always adhered to the scope of their actions, not daring to overstep the bounds, and only following the lead of the Japanese. Without the instigation of the Japanese, the Koreans would never have had the courage to riot so greatly. While speaking, he gesticulated and wept bitterly, urging compatriots from all walks of life to wake up together. Otherwise, the Japanese would gain ground and their harm would be unimaginable. The listeners were moved.

Shouting Loudly: Mr. Linken Youren, the director-general of the Foreign Aid Association for the Netherlands, said in his speech that China has a vast territory, abundant resources, and a large population. Compared with Japan, which has only three islands, it is like comparing heaven and earth. Today, the Japanese are so tyrannical and have no regard for China. If we continue to endure without devising countermeasures, it is tantamount to the death of the national spirit. There is no greater sorrow than the death of the heart. Today's matter, although nominally a Korean anti-Chinese movement, is actually a Japanese plot to annex China. Koreans are puppets of the Japanese and should be pitied for their ignorance and being used by others. To catch thieves, catch the king. We must deal with Japan with all our strength. He also listed the various inferior acts of the Japanese against China since Yuan Shikai proclaimed himself emperor and presented the Twenty-One Demands, hitting the table again and again with his hand, shouting loudly, excited and慷慨, making people excited.

The Rattlesnake of Qujiang 160

— Yi Mei

A guest from Qujiang in Lingnan told of the production of rattlesnakes in his area. The snake is very poisonous, seven or eight feet long, with a ring-shaped object at the end of its tail that can make a sound, a shrill sound like a cicada singing on a summer willow. It likes to eat lychees, winding among the trees, and those with many fruits are eaten to the end. It eats 300 lychees a day. Even Su Shi is inferior to its good fortune. In a certain year, when the lychees were ripe, there were many snakes. The owner of the orchard was worried and tried to feed cranes to eliminate them. The cranes were exhausted, and there was no way to recruit more. Some people used paper cranes to guard the lychees. The cranes ate the snakes, and the red top of the crown looked like blood poison accumulated there. A certain servant did not notice and touched it, and his wrist and elbow swelled up immediately, extending to the whole body and dying. Alas, the poison of the rattlesnake! The snake comes out at night. The guest prepared a hunting gun. Late at night, he heard the sound of a snake, happily pushed his pillow and got up. He went out to track the sound and shot it. Although it was dark and indistinguishable, he saw several tails lying stiff on the ground the next morning. The guest was familiar with marksmanship, so he was able to hit the target eight or nine times out of ten. When the guest talked about this, he raised his eyebrows and waved his arms, with the air of the pavilion chief of Sishang beheading the son of the White Emperor.

A Record of Zhuiyu Nan Yao 161

— Zhi

Mei Lanfang's trip to the south this time, time is easy, almost three months have passed. At the beginning, he was hired by Nantian and embarked on a journey to Zhuhai, performing twice in Hong Kong and Guangdong. Everyone was empty, no less than in those years. Since returning from the Americas, it was the first time to meet with the southern people. When he passed through Shanghai, he stayed at the Cangzhou Hotel for two days. He stayed in Hong Kong and Guangdong for 30 days before and after. He also took the opportunity to go to Zhongshan County to visit Cui Tingxiang and visit the Gongle Garden to see the construction and achievements of this model county. Then, he rushed to attend the ceremony of the Du Family Ancestral Hall and performed for three days. Mr. Yuesheng had the grand wish to set up a library to benefit the scholars, so he specially purchased 500 copies of the exquisite printed edition of the Guangya Congshu Complete Collection from Guangdong to donate to him. Mei is simple and elegant, and respects learning and admires the ancients. One is to observe the prosperity of the Du Family Hall, and the other is to promote the heart of benefiting the people. Both are commendable. When he came to Shanghai, he was hosted by the Du Family and stayed at the Central Hotel. After the performance, he was originally scheduled to return north. However, he traveled south in the past. He never had the opportunity to see the scenery of Jiangnan. He felt regretful. Coincidentally, he had a friend who invited him to visit the Holy Lake Yuhang together. He went to Hangzhou with Mr. Zhang Xiaolin and Du Yuesheng, as well as Mr. Wang Hu and other gentlemen. He stayed for several days and took a long-distance bus to Mogan Mountain. He went around to see the scenery. He turned to Yuhang and went to Dongxi Tianmu, where he explored the forests. He stayed in the temple for three days and respectfully drew Buddha statues to leave as a souvenir. He made offerings. The devotees and Buddhas were all very happy. The grandeur of the dragon and elephant was rare. When he returned from Hangzhou, it was already midsummer and he could not stay. However, the philanthropists of Shanghai, because Jiangxi was in urgent need of disaster relief, planned to raise money to help. Xiong Tianyi, the commander of the Shanghai garrison, also sent a telegram from Jiangxi, urging him to help the people of Jiangxi survive. Mei had the people in mind and was saddened by the news. He immediately agreed. So, he performed again at the Grand Stage for three days. 30,000 yuan was sold in tickets. The summer was hot and there were no empty seats. The Huahlau was 100 yuan, and the third floor was only about 1 yuan, which was unprecedented. It was the Shanghai people who were determined to do justice, and it was also the power of Mei's call. Mei is still young, and his appearance is not inferior to ten years ago. His voice is clearer and more durable, singing high into the clouds without any difficulty. Insiders believe that his voice is like this today, and it will not change throughout his life. This is a great blessing for those who appreciate music and coordinate rhythm. The day after the end of the performance, he put aside his business and hurriedly set off. Therefore, I wrote a short note on his itinerary to inform him, and also as a ticket for his return in the autumn.

Short message: Huang Hanhou, Guangling, is a young and handsome man who is proficient in four styles of calligraphy and is good at shallow engraving. He can engrave more than a thousand characters in an inch-square ivory card, as fine as mosquitoes' feet. He is especially good at engraving fans, with those who write the Former and Latter Chapters on Dispatching the Army and the Former and Latter Odes to the Red Cliff, and those who write the Preface to the Sacred Religion and the Preface to the Collection of the Orchid Pavilion and Thirteen Postscripts, each imitating its style, with vivid charm. The fan is no more than a foot long and only a few points wide, but the spacing is even and meticulous. Those with slightly dull eyesight cannot see the inscriptions and seals, which contain the four words "a lifetime of effort," without a microscope. It is said that on the 18th of this month, he will display hundreds of his carefully crafted works at the Ningbo Fellow Association 4 and open the exhibition for three days.

Statement: In yesterday's "He Han Er" manuscript, the 15th line has an empty lead, which is actually the word "mosquito". It was corrected in the proofs, but it was omitted temporarily. This is a special statement.

Rambling Talks About Touring Korea (6) 162

— Ji Ping

What Koreans feel most tragic is the high pressure of Japanese economic power in the past 20 years. Up to now, except for a few nobles and the bourgeoisie, the vast majority of the people feel the difficulty of life. The national economic strength is completely in the hands of the Japanese. No matter what skills you have, you cannot get rid of this restraint. Although it is not a natural formation, it cannot be recovered by human power. Alas, the tragedy of national subjugation. Koreans only now understand that it is a pain to the flesh. However, it is too late to regret. The productive capacity of Koreans is also weak. In the city, they cannot see a large company, large business, or large factory founded by themselves. In the Korean street in Seoul, only small businesses are seen, selling handmade household utensils. There are not many shops with capital of more than 1,000 yuan. The lively business districts, the prosperous markets, and the large capital businesses are completely concentrated in the Japanese street. Even the Chinese street business is very quiet. They have all been affected by Japanese economic aggression. If you want to describe the state of Koreans being economically oppressed, it is like a person who is terminally ill. It is in danger. Now, it is urgent for a good doctor to perform surgery and cure it from the root.

Korean customs are still conservative and have not been assimilated by the Japanese. For example, the four major needs of clothing, food, housing, and transportation, except for transportation, all rely on their own supply. The most special custom of Koreans is that they wear white clothes all year round. Men, old and young, are all the same. Some people say that this is not only their custom, but also contains the meaning of "never forget national humiliation". The long shirts worn by men are buttoned together in front of the chest and have two ties. White cloth socks and rubber shoes. The elderly also add a black hat. The skirts worn by women are very long, while the shirts only reach the waist. They are also buttoned together in front of the chest and tied a knot. Middle-aged women and above also wear a white cloth scarf. The clothing materials are mostly cotton woven white cloth. In summer, it is linen. Fashionable women only use white silk. Very few people wear Japanese kimonos and clogs. The intellectual class also wears Western clothes. Seeing that they are not particular about clothing, and most of the sources of clothing are local products. The main agricultural product of Korea is rice. A large amount of rice is exported to Japan every year. Their own food is supplied by the millet of the three northeastern provinces. Therefore, the Korean farmers who cultivate in the three provinces of Liaoning, Jilin, and Heilongjiang in our country transport a considerable amount of grain back to Korea every year. Korean cigarettes and alcohol are monopolized by the Governor-General's Office. Koreans have a deep love for this and therefore consume a lot. In the eyes of the Japanese, they believe that the profits and taxes from tobacco and alcohol are a huge source of income. Speaking of the housing problem of Koreans, it is worth studying. Try crossing the Tsushima Strait from Shimonoseki, Japan, to Busan, Korea, and taking the train all the way to Sinuiju. You can cross the Korean Peninsula in one day and night. The scene of the countryside along the way seems very desolate. The civilian houses are all small thatched huts with mud or reed walls. Occasionally, you can see a few white-walled tile houses, which are said to be the residences of Japanese people. Most of the people living in tile houses are landlords and capitalists. They have a great potential in the countryside, as if they have the right to command ordinary farmers. It can be seen that the power of the Japanese has penetrated deep into the hinterland and expanded to the people.

Rotary Club of Storytellers

？？？(23) 163

— Xu Zhuodai

So, after a year, the ink on the inkstone dried up. He ground it again, intending to continue working. Unexpectedly, the mistress, who was like a drama onstage, came upstairs again. When Ziliang looked, he couldn't help but feel a little strange. It turned out that she was holding a small child in her arms and was smiling at her husband.

"Look! Is this child good-looking?"

Ziliang, who had been married for three years without children, was really curious:

"Whose child is this?"

"Haha! This is my son. Don't you recognize him?"

As the mistress spoke, she turned the child's face towards Ziliang.

"Good child, call him 'Daddy'!"

Ziliang looked closely at the child's face and knew that it seemed to be the Wang family next door.

"What a joke! A father wouldn't recognize his own son."

As the mistress spoke, she sat on the chair, unbuttoned her chest, exposed her left breast, and put the nipple into the child's mouth:

"Good child! Eat!"

Ziliang found the mistress's actions a bit ridiculous. Unexpectedly, the child couldn't get any milk at that time, and he started to cry, and he was crying loudly. Ziliang couldn't help but say:

"Whose child is this? What are you doing bringing him over? He's crying! Hurry up and return him! Otherwise, if they hear us, they might not agree!"

The mistress also felt that there was nothing she could do. Although she was using her hand to tap on the edge of the desk, the child's crying still didn't stop. She had no choice but to carry him downstairs. There was already a knock on the front door.

Surge in Yarn and Cotton Yarn Prices 180

The yarn market is very strong, with a dramatic price surge. The atmosphere of economic severance with Japan is again tense. Speculators are swarming in, and buying sentiment is very high. The upward trend is sharp. Although there are large firms selling off, retail investors are uniformly absorbing the supply. At the same time, actual sales in the north are vigorous. Some are stockpiling for the rainy day due to the growing boycott movement. The spot market is very tight. Recent transactions in branded yarn have been substantial, with considerable strength on both the long and short sides. Future changes are likely to be significant.

Cotton Marker Jumps Three Taels 181

In the pre-market opening of the exchange's cotton market, the overseas cotton was flat and weak. However, the atmosphere in the market was very tight, and buying sentiment was strong. Prices rose by one to two taels for all months. Prices rose again in the second session, resulting in gains of 2.2, 2.4, 2.5, and 2.7 qian for all months. The upward trend was even stronger in the afternoon opening. There was pressure from large firms in the second and third sessions, causing a slight pullback. Near-term contracts only rose by 0.3, 0.6, and 0.8 qian, while distant contracts were flat. Transactions totaled 83,650 bales sold. Dafu sold 1,600 bales, Yuda sold 1,200 bales, Daji sold 1,150 bales, Shenchang sold 1,150 bales, Hengde sold 2,150 bales, Yichang sold 4,600 bales, Xincheng sold 4,750 bales, Gongtai sold 1,350 bales, Taixing sold 1,200 bales, and Ruidai sold 1,400 bales. Minghua bought 1,250 bales, Heshen bought 2,650 bales, Rongxing bought 5,800 bales, Shunda bought 2,200 bales, Changfeng bought 4,900 bales, Tianlong bought 1,050 bales, Yiyu bought 1,150 bales, and Jifeng bought 1,000 bales. The closing prices for the cotton market are recorded below.

Excellent Customer Sales of Spot Yarn 182

Spot yarn sales remain robust. A total of 4,850 bales were purchased by various firms throughout the day, and dealers acquired 1,100 bales. Prices rose significantly by 2 to 3 taels. Guangdong customers bought 290 bales, inland customers bought 1,210 bales, Sichuan customers bought 450 bales, Tianjin customers bought 1,300 bales, Shantou customers bought 400 bales, northern customers bought 300 bales, and miscellaneous customers bought 250 bales.

Cotton Prices Surge by Half a Tael 183

The cotton market is tightening. Although the situation for American cotton is still weak, the local conditions in Shanghai are affected by reports of continuous mold and rain and alleged damage to cotton in Shaanxi. Gold prices fluctuate sharply, making it difficult to predict. Therefore, market conditions are mixed. Japanese firms are tightly holding onto new, distant cotton contracts. The overall trend is still flat and soft. Progress depends on news regarding new cotton and American cotton.

Domestic Cotton Follows Yarn Market 184

In the pre-market opening of the exchange's domestic cotton market, the overseas cotton was flat, but the yarn market rose, driving up cotton prices. Prices rose by 2 to 3 qian for all months. In the afternoon, near-term contracts rose by 2.5 qian, while distant contracts were flat. Transactions totaled 49,500 dan. Yuande sold 3,800 dan, and Jifeng sold 1,000 dan. Dachang sold 1,400 dan. Changfeng bought 5,100 dan, Yongda bought 2,800 dan, and Yichang bought 2,000 dan. The closing prices for the domestic cotton market are listed below.

Overseas Yarn Remains on a Downward Trend

Egyptian cotton spot prices rose by ten points. Indian cotton firmed due to short covering and good news from Germany.
